Merkel also remarked that she would be "thankful" if the countries could strengthen cooperation "in all areas".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Spain" title="Prime Minister of Spain">Spanish Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Mariano_Rajoy" title="Mariano Rajoy">Mariano Rajoy</a>, who has a close relationship with Macri, congratulated him and invited him to carry out a state visit "as soon as possible", stating that he is confident that the new government will "lead this new stage with success" while offering "the necessary support to consolidate the historical ties of friendship, fraternity and cooperation". The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Argentina-Spain_relations" title="Argentina-Spain relations">relationship between Spain and Argentina</a> had become increasingly tense under the presidency of Cristina Kirchner, particularly after the <a href="/wiki/Renationalization_of_YPF" title="Renationalization of YPF">Renationalization of YPF</a> in 2012.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129"><a href="#cite_note-129">[129]</a></sup> In a telegram to Macri, <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">Russian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> expressed his hopes that the two countries will continue to increase the "bilateral cooperation within diverse areas and the coordination of efforts to resolve current occurrences within the international agenda", adding that "the fundamental interests of the people of Russia and Argentina contribute to guarantee the stability and security of <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">Latin America</a> and the world", while reminding Macri that the countries had recently celebrated <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Argentina-Russia_relations" title="Argentina-Russia relations">130 years of diplomatic relations</a>. Putin also made reference to the ongoing <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_power" title="Nuclear power">nuclear power</a> and hydrocarbon extraction projects between the countries.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130"><a href="#cite_note-130">[130]</a></sup> In February 2016, Macri received the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Bulgaria" title="President of Bulgaria">President of Bulgaria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rosen_Plevneliev" title="Rosen Plevneliev">Rosen Plevneliev</a>, at the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a> in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>. Both leaders spoke of investments in each country; Plevneliev also met with entrepreneurs and visited the <a href="/wiki/National_Congress_of_Argentina" title="National Congress of Argentina">National Congress</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131"><a href="#cite_note-131">[131]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:211px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1793" data-file-width="2267" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg/209px-Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg/314px-Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg/418px-Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg 2x" width="209"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Matteo_Renzi_and_Mauricio_Macri_in_2016.jpeg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri with Italian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Matteo_Renzi" title="Matteo Renzi">Matteo Renzi</a>, in 2016.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Italy" title="Prime Minister of Italy">Italian Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Matteo_Renzi" title="Matteo Renzi">Matteo Renzi</a> called Macri on the night of his victory and stated that he would meet soon with the new president to "open a new page of collaboration between the two countries". He also highlighted the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Italian_Argentine" title="Italian Argentine">historical and cultural ties</a> between the two countries, stating that "it is the country with the largest presence of Italian citizens in the world", numbering some 900,000. The <a href="/wiki/Cambiemos" title="Cambiemos">Cambiemos</a> victory also provoked much reaction in the domestic Italian press.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Piqu.C3.A9_132-0"><a href="#cite_note-Piqu.C3.A9-132">[132]</a></sup> On 15 February 2016, Renzi met with Macri for a two-day state visit to <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>;<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133"><a href="#cite_note-133">[133]</a></sup> Renzi was the first European leader to meet Macri after the <a href="/wiki/Argentine_general_election,_2015" title="Argentine general election, 2015">2015 presidential election</a> and the first Italian Prime Minister since <a href="/wiki/Romano_Prodi" title="Romano Prodi">Romano Prodi</a> in 1998 to visit Argentina.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134"><a href="#cite_note-134">[134]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:212px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2947" data-file-width="3472" height="178" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg/210px-Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg/315px-Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg/420px-Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg 2x" width="210"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Macri_with_Putin_G20_2016_02.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri with the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President of Russia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a>, September 2016.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">French President</a> <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande" title="François Hollande">François Hollande</a> sent a telegram to Macri and expressed "We will have the opportunity at that time to deepen our dialogue and our bilateral relationship that is one of the densest known to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Latin_American" title="Latin American">Latin American</a> continent". Hollande also confirmed a state visit to Argentina in February 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135"><a href="#cite_note-135">[135]</a></sup> Upon congratulating President Macri on his victory in the 2015 election, President Hollande announced that he would visit Argentina in February 2016. During his state visit to Buenos Aires on 24–25 February 2016, Macri and Hollande signed 20 bilateral agreements.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136"><a href="#cite_note-136">[136]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">British Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> called Macri after his election to congratulate him and offer his support for his presidency. A <a href="/wiki/Downing_Street" title="Downing Street">Downing Street</a> spokesperson stated that "both leaders expect to meet in the near future", emphasising trade relations and investments, while also prioritising the establishment of a free trade agreement between <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MERCOSUR" title="MERCOSUR">MERCOSUR</a> and the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> "as soon as possible".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137"><a href="#cite_note-137">[137]</a></sup> The chancellor <a href="/wiki/Susana_Malcorra" title="Susana Malcorra">Susana Malcorra</a> clarified that Argentina would maintain the Argentine claim in the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands_sovereignty_dispute" title="Falkland Islands sovereignty dispute">Falkland Islands sovereignty dispute</a>, but would also try to expand the <a href="/wiki/Argentina%E2%80%93United_Kingdom_relations" title="Argentina–United Kingdom relations">Argentina–United Kingdom relations</a> into other areas of interest.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138"><a href="#cite_note-138">[138]</a></sup> Macri met Cameron at the <a href="/wiki/World_Economic_Forum" title="World Economic Forum">World Economic Forum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Davos" title="Davos">Davos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, to which Argentina officially returned after 12 years. After the meeting, Macri said he had a "very nice meeting" with Cameron and explained in a brief meeting with journalists that their goal is to initiate "a relationship in which all issues on the table are placed under one umbrella". Chancellor Malcorra reported that the dispute over the sovereignty of the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a> was one of the most important axes of the meeting, but not the only one. "Focusing our relationship only in the Islands is to stay with the glass half full," said the minister.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139"><a href="#cite_note-139">[139]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:211px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Macri_Hollande2.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3278" data-file-width="4917" height="139" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Macri_Hollande2.jpg/209px-Macri_Hollande2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Macri_Hollande2.jpg/314px-Macri_Hollande2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Macri_Hollande2.jpg/418px-Macri_Hollande2.jpg 2x" width="209"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Macri_Hollande2.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri with the <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande" title="François Hollande">François Hollande</a> in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In July 2016, President Macri started a European tour that took him to <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> and <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, where he sought to project his international leadership as a political and commercial partner of the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>.Macri held in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> a meeting with French President <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Francois_Hollande" title="Francois Hollande">Francois Hollande</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a> with German Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a>, in this case in the context of a two-day official visit in which the President was accompanied by businessmen. In addition to meeting with the two leaders brunt of the European Union, Macri was received in Brussels by the European Council President <a href="/wiki/Donald_Tusk" title="Donald Tusk">Donald Tusk</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_Representative_of_the_European_Union_for_Foreign_Affairs" title="High Representative of the European Union for Foreign Affairs">High Representative of the European Union for Foreign Affairs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Federica_Mogherini" title="Federica Mogherini">Federica Mogherini</a>, and by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/King_Philip_of_Belgium" title="King Philip of Belgium">King Philip</a> and <a href="/wiki/Queen_Mathilde_of_Belgium" title="Queen Mathilde of Belgium">Queen Mathilde</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Palace_of_Brussels" title="Royal Palace of Brussels">Royal Palace of Brussels</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140"><a href="#cite_note-140">[140]</a></sup></p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Asia">Asia</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:211px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2044" data-file-width="2924" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg/209px-Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg/314px-Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg/418px-Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg 2x" width="209"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Macri_with_Xi_Jinping_G20_2016_01.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri with the <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="President of the People's Republic of China">President of China</a>, <a href="/wiki/Xi_Jinping" title="Xi Jinping">Xi Jinping</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2016_G20_Hangzhou_summit" title="2016 G20 Hangzhou summit">2016 G20 summit</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>On March 27, 2016, a <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a> official announced that President Macri will meet with Chinese president <a href="/wiki/Xi_Jinping" title="Xi Jinping">Xi Jinping</a> on 1 April in the framework of the <a href="/wiki/2016_Nuclear_Security_Summit" title="2016 Nuclear Security Summit">2016 Nuclear Security Summit</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_D.C." title="Washington D.C.">Washington D.C.</a>. <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> and <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> established diplomatic relations in 1972 but revived especially during the mandates of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nestor_Kirchner" title="Nestor Kirchner">Nestor Kirchner</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cristina_Kirchner" title="Cristina Kirchner">Cristina Kirchner</a>, during which relations reached the level of "Comprehensive Strategic Partnership". However, since the assumption of Macri, the relationship was observed for the promises of the now head of state during the election campaign to "review" the proceedings between the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a> and <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a> between 2003 and 2015. Both countries signed agreements in 2015 for the construction of two new nuclear power plants in Argentina, with a total investment of 15,000 million dollars in an operation in which China pledged 85 percent of funding. <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> is the second main destination of Argentine exports after <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141"><a href="#cite_note-141">[141]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-142"><a href="#cite_note-142">[142]</a></sup></p>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/2016_Nuclear_Security_Summit" title="2016 Nuclear Security Summit">2016 Nuclear Security Summit</a> Macri also met with Japanese prime minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shinzo_Abe" title="Shinzo Abe">Shinzo Abe</a>, Indian prime minister <a href="/wiki/Narendra_Modi" title="Narendra Modi">Narendra Modi</a> and South Korean president <a href="/wiki/Park_Geun-hye" title="Park Geun-hye">Park Geun-hye</a> with the aim to resume relations and try to add investors in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>. <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> have a strong interest in investing in the areas of mining, energy, and infrastructure, and to raise levels of trade with <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>. It is also known that there is a strong interest of Japanese and Korean companies to invest in the lithium deposits of the <a href="/wiki/Argentine_Northwest" title="Argentine Northwest">Argentine Northwest</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-143"><a href="#cite_note-143">[143]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Macri_%26_Abe.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2996" data-file-width="2389" height="251" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Macri_%26_Abe.jpg/200px-Macri_%26_Abe.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Macri_%26_Abe.jpg/300px-Macri_%26_Abe.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Macri_%26_Abe.jpg/400px-Macri_%26_Abe.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Macri_%26_Abe.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri with Japanese prime minister <a href="/wiki/Shinz%C5%8D_Abe" title="Shinzō Abe">Shinzō Abe</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a> in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>, November 2016.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>In September 2016, during the <a href="/wiki/2016_G20_Hangzhou_summit" title="2016 G20 Hangzhou summit">G20 summit</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hangzhou" title="Hangzhou">Hangzhou</a>, <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>, President Macri met with Indian prime minister <a href="/wiki/Narendra_Modi" title="Narendra Modi">Narendra Modi</a> and they made a commitment to expand the <a href="/wiki/Argentina%E2%80%93India_relations" title="Argentina–India relations">relations between Argentina and India</a>. "I think so far the relationship between our countries has been a little superficial. It's a good opportunity to deepen" Macri said. Macri met Modi in one of the last added to its agenda of activities at the G20 summit bilateral meetings. Macri expressed interest to "increase and diversify" Argentine exports to India and for Indian companies to "come to invest in our country." Modi also expressed satisfaction that the Confederation of Indian Industry will participate in the Business Forum in the city of <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>. In addition, the Argentine president exchanged a greeting with Indonesian president <a href="/wiki/Joko_Widodo" title="Joko Widodo">Joko Widodo</a>. In both meetings Macri was accompanied by Foreign Minister <a href="/wiki/Susana_Malcorra" title="Susana Malcorra">Susana Malcorra</a>, Economy Minister <a href="/wiki/Alfonso_Prat-Gay" title="Alfonso Prat-Gay">Alfonso Prat-Gay</a>, and Secretary of Strategic Affairs Fulvio Pompeo.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144"><a href="#cite_note-144">[144]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup></p>
<p>In November 2016, President Macri received Japanese prime minister <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shinzo_Abe" title="Shinzo Abe">Shinzo Abe</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a> of <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a> to give a new impetus to the economic and commercial <a href="/wiki/Argentina%E2%80%93Japan_relations" title="Argentina–Japan relations">relations between both nations</a>. Abe's state visit to <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> was the first of a Japanese leader in 57 years. Macri and Abe signed several bilateral instruments, including a Memorandum of Cooperation for the establishment of an enhanced mechanism for political consultations. The last precedent was in 1959, when <a href="/wiki/Nobusuke_Kishi" title="Nobusuke Kishi">Nobusuke Kishi</a>, Abe's grandfather, arrived to hold a bilateral meeting with the then President <a href="/wiki/Arturo_Frondizi" title="Arturo Frondizi">Arturo Frondizi</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup></p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_East">Middle East</span></h4>
<p>On December 21, government lawyers withdrew an appeal in Federal Court made by Macri's predecessor, Cristina Fernández de Kirchner, over the constitutionality of a <a href="/wiki/Memorandum_of_understanding_between_Argentina_and_Iran" title="Memorandum of understanding between Argentina and Iran">memorandum</a> she had signed with the Iranian government, to investigate the 1994 <a href="/wiki/AMIA_bombing" title="AMIA bombing">AMIA bombing</a>. The memorandum was criticized by both Israel and Argentina's Jewish community, as Iran was long suspected of being involved in the attack. The memorandum had been ruled unconstitutional by a federal court during Kirchner's administration, and along with the withdrawal of the appeal, the memorandum was voided by Macri's administration. The move was praised by Israeli Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> as an improvement of <a href="/wiki/Argentina%E2%80%93Israel_relations" title="Argentina–Israel relations">bilateral relations</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup></p>
<p>On July 2016 President Macri met with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emir_of_Qatar" title="Emir of Qatar">Emir of Qatar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tamim_bin_Hamad_Al_Thani" title="Tamim bin Hamad Al Thani">Tamim bin Hamad Al Thani</a>, at the <a href="/wiki/Quinta_de_Olivos" title="Quinta de Olivos">Presidential Residence of Olivos</a>. Both led the signing of memorandums of understanding signed Chancellor, <a href="/wiki/Susana_Malcorra" title="Susana Malcorra">Susana Malcorra</a>, and his Qatari counterpart, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Mohammed_bin_Abdulrahman_bin_Jassim_Al-Thani&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Mohammed bin Abdulrahman bin Jassim Al-Thani (page does not exist)">Mohammed bin Abdulrahman bin Jassim Al-Thani</a>. also they attended by the Chief of Staff, <a href="/wiki/Marcos_Pe%C3%B1a" title="Marcos Peña">Marcos Peña</a>, and the Minister of Finance and Public Finance, <a href="/wiki/Alfonso_Prat-Gay" title="Alfonso Prat-Gay">Alfonso Prat-Gay</a>. In 2015, <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> exported to <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a> goods by 11.5 million dollars and imported worth just over 153 million dollars, what, 141 million deficit in bilateral balance totaled 164 million, down 35 percent in relation to 2014, when the exchange was 471.5 million dollars, according to statistics from the <a href="/wiki/Inter-American_Development_Bank" title="Inter-American Development Bank">Inter-American Development Bank</a> (IDB).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Economic_policy">Economic policy</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:217px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3232" data-file-width="4928" height="141" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg/215px-MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg/323px-MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg/430px-MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg 2x" width="215"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MM_Clinton_Global_Initiative.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri alongside President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a>, Italian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Matteo_Renzi" title="Matteo Renzi">Matteo Renzi</a>, economist <a href="/wiki/Ngozi_Okonjo-Iweala" title="Ngozi Okonjo-Iweala">Ngozi Okonjo-Iweala</a> and London Mayor <a href="/wiki/Sadiq_Khan" title="Sadiq Khan">Sadiq Khan</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Clinton_Global_Initiative" title="Clinton Global Initiative">Clinton Global Initiative</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>One of the first changes to economic policy from the Macri administration was to, just seven days after Macri had taken office, remove the <a href="/wiki/Argentine_currency_controls_(2011%E2%80%9315)" title="Argentine currency controls (2011–15)">currency controls</a> that had been in place for four consecutive years.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150"><a href="#cite_note-150">[150]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151"><a href="#cite_note-151">[151]</a></sup> The move signified a 30% <a href="/wiki/Devaluation" title="Devaluation">devaluation</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Argentine_peso" title="Argentine peso">peso</a>, and was met with both criticism and praise.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup></p>
<p>In December 2015, Macri's administration removed taxes on exports of grain, beef and fish, while keeping a 30% export tax on soy, down 5% from a previous rate of 35%.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup> The administration also did away with previously imposed quotas on grain exports.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup></p>
<p>On January 19, 2016, Macri attended the <a href="/wiki/World_Economic_Forum" title="World Economic Forum">World Economic Forum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Davos" title="Davos">Davos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> with <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Massa" title="Sergio Massa">Sergio Massa</a> and part of his <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cabinet_of_Mauricio_Macri" title="Cabinet of Mauricio Macri">cabinet</a>, looking for investments. He had meetings with various business representatives, politicians and journalists. Some of them were <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_Vice_President" title="US Vice President">US Vice President</a> <a href="/wiki/Joe_Biden" title="Joe Biden">Joe Biden</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a>, <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a>, the founder of Virgin Group <a href="/wiki/Richard_Branson" title="Richard Branson">Richard Branson</a>, CEO of <a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a> <a href="/wiki/Eric_Schmidt" title="Eric Schmidt">Eric Schmidt</a>, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Queen_of_the_Netherlands" title="Queen of the Netherlands">Queen of the Netherlands</a>, and the President and CEO <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coca_Cola" title="Coca Cola">Coca Cola</a>, <a href="/wiki/Muhtar_Kent" title="Muhtar Kent">Muhtar Kent</a>, among others.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup> It was the first time that <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> participated in the Forum since 2003. The last president to attend was <a href="/wiki/Eduardo_Duhalde" title="Eduardo Duhalde">Eduardo Duhalde</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup></p>
<p>One of Macri's promises during the campaign was the elimination of the <a href="/wiki/Income_tax" title="Income tax">income tax</a> for workers. He said, "During my government workers will not pay tax on profits".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Economy_and_Public_Finances_(Argentina)" title="Ministry of Economy and Public Finances (Argentina)">Minister of the Economy and Public Finances</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alfonso_Prat-Gay" title="Alfonso Prat-Gay">Alfonso Prat-Gay</a> said that the draft amendments to the income tax would be sent to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Congress_of_Argentina" title="Congress of Argentina">Congress</a> for treatment.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup></p>
<p>In March 2016, after holding a bilateral meeting at <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a>, the U.S. president, <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> defined Macri as a "key ally" in the region and called for a bilateral working group to eliminate trade barriers. After this visit, the idea of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Free_trade_area" title="Free trade area">free trade</a> is in the crosshairs of the US and Argentina.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> hosted the Argentina Business &amp; Investment Forum in <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a> from September 12–14, 2016. The event was highlight Argentina’s determination to attract <a href="/wiki/Foreign_direct_investment" title="Foreign direct investment">foreign direct investment</a> as part of its path towards long-term and inclusive economic growth.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Forum was a major milestone in the implementation of President Macri business and investment reforms, which seek to attract <a href="/wiki/Foreign_direct_investment" title="Foreign direct investment">foreign direct investment</a> in each of the next four years. Attracting leading figures from the private and public sector, the Argentina Business &amp; Investment Forum will present a clear and ambitious vision for <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>’s future and position the country as an attractive destination on the global investment map.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163"><a href="#cite_note-163">[163]</a></sup></p>
<p>Announcing the Forum, President Macri described the event as an opportunity to lay out the strategies for invigorating the country’s key <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Argentina" title="Economy of Argentina">economic sectors</a> and presenting attractive opportunities to local, regional, and global investors. <i>“Argentina has decided to take its place in the global landscape. We need global companies to invest in our high-potential energy, agribusiness, technology and communications sectors as well as finance and construct roads and ports. Argentina offers one of the most attractive investment opportunities in the world over the next decade,”</i> said President Macri.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164"><a href="#cite_note-164">[164]</a></sup></p>
<p>The Forum served as a platform for discussions, debates, presentations and high-level meetings between Argentinean business and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">government leaders</a> and international investors and partners, with the goal of stimulating <a href="/wiki/Foreign_direct_investment" title="Foreign direct investment">foreign direct investment</a> into the country and securing public-private partnerships.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Political_views">Political views</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Syrian_refugees">Syrian refugees</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:MacriONU01.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2220" data-file-width="2734" height="179" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/MacriONU01.jpg/220px-MacriONU01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/MacriONU01.jpg/330px-MacriONU01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/MacriONU01.jpg/440px-MacriONU01.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:MacriONU01.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Macri deliver his first speech at <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>President Macri has said he intends to allow more than 3,000 <a href="/wiki/Refugees_of_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Refugees of the Syrian Civil War">Syrian refugees</a> to resettle in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>. The Argentine government and the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> (EU) are negotiating an agreement in order for Argentina to receive around 3,000 Syrian refugees.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> will be the first country in the world to help the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> solve the greatest refugee crisis since <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>. The statement was released during President Macri’s official tour through <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a>. Talks of Argentina helping the Syrian refugees occurred during a meeting the president with the European Union’s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/High_Representative_for_Foreign_Affairs_and_Security_Policy" title="High Representative for Foreign Affairs and Security Policy">High Representative for Foreign Affairs and Security Policy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Federica_Mogherini" title="Federica Mogherini">Federica Mogherini</a>, in the offices of the European Commission in <a href="/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="LGBT_rights">LGBT rights</span></h3>
<p>Macri announced his personal support for <a href="/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_Argentina" title="Same-sex marriage in Argentina">same-sex marriage</a> and <a href="/wiki/LGBT_adoption" title="LGBT adoption">adoption for LGBT couples</a>, and outlined plans to pursue the issue in early 2009. "The world is going in this direction. We have to live with and accept this reality. I hope they are happy," said Macri when he decided to not appeal the ruling that enabled two men to marry civilly. It was during his tenure as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chief_of_Government_of_Buenos_Aires" title="Chief of Government of Buenos Aires">Mayor of Buenos Aires</a> that the first gay marriage in <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">Latin America</a> was performed in the city.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup> Because of this support, it began a tense relationship between Macri, and former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Archbishop_of_Buenos_Aires" title="Archbishop of Buenos Aires">Archbishop of Buenos Aires</a>, Jorge Bergoglio, now <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> because, unlike Macri, he was strongly opposed to the enactment of the Act for same sex marriage in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170"><a href="#cite_note-170">[170]</a></sup> Current <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chief_of_Government_of_Buenos_Aires" title="Chief of Government of Buenos Aires">Chief of Government of Buenos Aires</a>, <a href="/wiki/Horacio_Rodr%C3%ADguez_Larreta" title="Horacio Rodríguez Larreta">Horacio Rodríguez Larreta</a> said "Macri installed the discussion of equal marriage" in the country and described him as a person "with strong positions for sexual diversity".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171"><a href="#cite_note-171">[171]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Abortion">Abortion</span></h3>
<p>Macri has expressed views <a href="/wiki/Anti-abortion_movements" title="Anti-abortion movements">in opposition to abortion</a>. In an interview published by <i><a href="/wiki/La_Naci%C3%B3n" title="La Nación">La Nación</a></i> in 2014, he stated: "I am in favor of life; I don't think we need to open that debate".<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172"><a href="#cite_note-172">[172]</a></sup> Nevertheless, he clarified that he would abide by any law on the matter sanctioned by Congress, regardless of his personal views.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173"><a href="#cite_note-173">[173]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Indigenous_peoples">Indigenous peoples</span></h3>
<p>On December 16 Macri met with members of the <a href="/wiki/Toba_people" title="Toba people">Qom</a> community and 30 other ethnic groups of indigenous peoples. The meeting was held at the Museum of the Bicentennial of the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Government House</a> and the delegation was headed by the leader of the Qom community, <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9lix_D%C3%ADaz_(cacique)" title="Félix Díaz (cacique)">Felix Diaz</a>. Macri said recognition of indigenous communities and support for policies regarding indigenous peoples are state policies during his government as President.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174"><a href="#cite_note-174">[174]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cabinet">Cabinet</span></h2>
<p>On the following days of the election, Macri and his team revealed the composition of the future cabinet. The cabinet was fully new, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/Lino_Bara%C3%B1ao" title="Lino Barañao">Lino Barañao</a>, who will continue as Minister of Science and Technology, having occupied the office since 2007 under <a href="/wiki/Cristina_Fern%C3%A1ndez_de_Kirchner" title="Cristina Fernández de Kirchner">Cristina Fernández de Kirchner</a> administration.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175"><a href="#cite_note-175">[175]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ancestry">Ancestry</span></h2>
